%.obj : %.asm
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\masm.rc:49
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	%do start_timing name=atime
	%if !%dir($(ASM_HACK_DIR))
	@-mkdir $(ASM_HACK_DIR)
	@%set REV_MDIRS =
	%foreach mdir $(APATH)
	@%set REV_MDIRS := $(mdir) $(REV_MDIRS)
	%end
	%foreach mdir $(REV_MDIRS)
	@%set copyfiles = $(mdir)\*.inc
	%foreach f $(copyfiles,*f)
	@copy $f $(ASM_HACK_DIR)\$(f,F) >$(ASM_HACK_DUMMY)
	%end
	%end
	%endif
	%if %exists($@)
	$(eko1)	$(@,F) \<-- $(?,F)
	%else
	$(eko1)	$(@,F) \<-- nonexistent
	%endif
	%if "$($(HLT)_ASFLAGS)" || '$($(.SOURCE,F)_ASFLAGS)'
	$(eko2) special flags = $($(HLT)_ASFLAGS) $($(.SOURCE,F)_ASFLAGS)
	%endif
	%if "$($(HLT)_ASDEFINES)" || "$($(.SOURCE,F)_ASDEFINES)"
	@%set D1 := $($(HLT)_ASDEFINES,M^\+,S'^\+'/D') $($(HLT)_ASDEFINES,M^[^-+],</D) $((HLT)_ASDEFINES,M^\-,S'^\-'/U')
	@%set D2 := $($(.SOURCE,F)_ASDEFINES,M^\+,S'^\+'/D') $($(.SOURCE,F)_ASDEFINES,M^[^-+],</D) $($(.SOURCE,F)_ASDEFINES,M^\-,S'^\-'/U')
	$(eko2) special defines = $(D1) $(D2)
	%endif
	$(@?3)%setenv ML=$(ASFLAGS) $(D1) $(D2) $($(HLT)_ASFLAGS) $($(.SOURCE,F)_ASFLAGS) /Fo$(ASM_HACK_DUMMY) $(ASM_HACK_DIR,</I) $(CONFIG_ADIRS,</I)
	@copy $< $(ASM_HACK_DIR) >$(ASM_HACK_DUMMY)
	@%set hack_name $(ASM_HACK_DIR)\$(<,F)
	$(@?2)$($(ASM)_ASM) $(hack_name)
	@(chdir $(ASM_HACK_DIR); gronkobj $(ASM_HACK_DUMMY,F) $@ $(hack_name) $<)
	%do end_timing vol=2 str="time:" name=atime

comp_h :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:229
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	@%set outfile = $(MAKETOP)\$(SYS)\$(h_out,F)
	$(eko2) Making $(outfile).
	%echo /* This File Automatically Generated by the build system */ > $(outfile)
	%echo $(h_pre) >> $(outfile)
	%echo #ifndef __$(h_out,F,UC,.=_) >>$(outfile)
	%echo #define  __$(h_out,F,UC,.=_) >>$(outfile)
	%foreach h_file $(h_in)
	$(@?3)cstrip -b -c $(h_file) >>$(outfile)
	%end
	%foreach inc_file $(inc_in)
	$(@?3)inc2h $(inc_file) $(outfile)
	%end
	%echo #endif /* __$(h_out,F,UC,.=_) */ >>$(outfile)

comp_inc :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:248
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	@%set outfile = $(MAKETOP)\$(SYS)\$(COMP)\$(ASM)\$(inc_out,F)
	$(eko2) Making $(outfile).
	@%echo $(inc_pre) >$(outfile)
	@%echo ifndef __$(inc_out,F,UC,.=_) >>$(outfile)
	@%echo __$(inc_out,F,UC,.=_) equ 1 >>$(outfile)
	%foreach i_file $(inc_in)
	$(@?3)cat $(i_file) >>$(outfile)
	%end
	@echo endif ;!__$(inc_out,F,UC,.=_) >>$(outfile)

compile_rule :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\complink.rc:103
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	%do start_timing name=ctime
	%if %exists($(target))
	$(eko1) $(target,F) \<-- $(?,F)
	%else
	$(eko1) $(target,F) \<-- nonexistent
	%endif
	%do gen_RULE arg1="$(source,F)"
	%do oneopt_RULE arg1="$(source,F)" arg2=$(HLT)
	%if "$($(HLT)_CFLAGS)" || "$(spec_CFLAGS)"
	$(eko2) special cflags = $($(HLT)_CFLAGS) $(spec_CFLAGS)
	%endif
	%if %null($(HLT)_PRECOMP_OBJS) && "$(PRECOMP)"
	@%set $(HLT)_PRECOMP_OBJS = $($(HLT)_OBJS)
	$(eko3) Precompiled headers will be used for all objs.
	%endif
	%if !"$(spec_cflags)" && "$(PRECOMP)" && '$($(HLT)_PRECOMP_OBJS,M$(target,R,F))'
	@%set TMP_IFILE = $(includefileflag)=lgpch.h
	@%set IFLAGS = $(precompflag)=$(@,d,>\lgpch.pch)
	%echo Precompiled headers will be used
	@%set PCLOC = $(@,d,>\lgpch.pch)
	%else
	%if ($(VENDOR)==watcom)
	@%set TMP_IFILE = $($(COMP)_IFILES,<$(includefileflag)\=)
	%else
	@%set TMP_IFILE = $($(COMP)_IFILES,<$(includefileflag))
	%endif
	@%set IFLAGS=
	%endif
	%if "$($(HLT)_DEFINES)" || "$($(source,F)_DEFINES)"
	@%set D1 := $($(HLT)_DEFINES,M^\+,S'^\+'/D') $($(HLT)_DEFINES,M^[^-+],</D) $((HLT)_DEFINES,M^\-,S'^\-'/U')
	@%set D2 := $($(source,F)_DEFINES,M^\+,S'^\+'/D') $($(source,F)_DEFINES,M^[^-+],</D) $($(source,F)_DEFINES,M^\-,S'^\-'/U')
	$(eko2) special defines = $(D1) $(D2)
	%endif
	$(@?3)%setenv $(envar)=$(IFLAGS) $(USER_CFLAGS) $($(HLT)_CFLAGS) $(spec_CFLAGS) $(DEFINES,</D) $(D1) $(D2) $(includeflag)=$(IPATH,W$(sp)$(includesep)) $(TMP_IFILE)  $(outputflag)$@
	$(@?2)$(compiler) $(source)
	%do end_timing vol=2 str="time:" name=ctime

config.mh :
    attributes: .ALWAYS .NOCOMPARE

copy_iff_changed :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:180
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	%if ! %exists ($(destfile))
	$(eko2)	$(destfile,S'^$(SB)'') not found.
	$(@?1)cp $(srcfile) $(destfile)
	$(@?3)chmod +w $(destfile)
	$(@?3)touch $(destfile)
	$(@?3)chmod -w $(destfile)
	%else
	@%set s1 = $(TMPDIR)\ciffc.s1
	@sum $(destfile) > $(s1)
	@%set s2 = $(TMPDIR)\ciffc.s2
	@sum $(srcfile) > $(s2)
	%if $(s1,@,1) != $(s2,@,1) || $(s1,@,2) != $(s2,@,2)
	$(eko2)	$(srcfile,.\\=) is changed, updating $(destfile)
	$(@?3)chmod +w $(destfile)
	@del $(destfile)
	$(@?1) cp $(srcfile) $(destfile)
	$(@?3)chmod +w $(destfile)
	$(@?3)touch $(destfile)
	$(@?3)chmod -w $(destfile)
	%else
	$(eko2) $(srcfile,.\\=) and $(destfile,S'^$(SB,\\=\\)\\'',.\\=) are the same, not updating.
	%endif
	%endif

deltmp :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:141
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	$(eko2) Deleting temporary files in $(TMPDIR).
	%if '$(TMPDIR)' && '$(VOLUME)' < 4
	@%set delfiles = $(TMPDIR)\*.*
	%foreach f $(delfiles,*f)
	@del $f
	%end
	%if $(SB)==$(PRJBACK)
	%if '$(PRECOMP)'
	%if (-e $(PCLOC))
	@del $(PCLOC)
	%endif
	%endif
	%endif
	@rmdir $(TMPDIR)
	%endif

do_check_sb :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\init.rc:96
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	%if %null(SB)
	%do deltmp
	%abort 0 "No sandbox; set SB.
	%endif
	@%set u = $(MAKETOP,S'\\' ')
	@%set t = $(SB,S'\\' ')
	%while '$t' != ''
	%if '$(t,1)' != '$(u,1)'
	%do deltmp
	%abort 0 "Current directory $(MAKETOP) not in sandbox $(SB)."
	%else
	@%set t = $(t,2,S'\\' ')
	@%set u = $(u,2,S'\\' ')
	%endif
	%end

do_net_map : last_drive
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\init.rc:185
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE

do_obj_map : last_drive
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\init.rc:147
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	%if ! (-e $(CWD,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(MAKETOP,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if  '$(lastdrive):' >= '$(OBJDRV,Z)' && '$(lastdrive):' >= '$(MAKETOP,Z)'
	%if %exists($(OBJDRV)\)
	$(@?3)--subst $(OBJDRV) /D
	%endif
	$(@?2)subst $(OBJDRV) $(MAKETOP,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))
	%elseif  '$(lastdrive):' >= '$(OBJDRV,Z)'
	%if %exists($(OBJDRV)\)
	$(@?3)--map rem $(OBJDRV) $(@eout3)
	$(@?3)--subst $(OBJDRV) /D
	%endif
	$(@?2)map root $(OBJDRV) = $(MAKETOP,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))
	%elseif  '$(lastdrive):' < '$(OBJDRV,Z)' && '$(lastdrive):' < '$(MAKETOP,Z)'
	%if %exists($(OBJDRV)\)
	$(@?3)--map rem $(OBJDRV) $(@eout3)
	%endif
	$(@?2)map root $(OBJDRV) = $(MAKETOP,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG)) $(@eout3)
	%else
	%do deltmp
	%abort 0 Illegal mapping requested.
	%endif

do_oth_dirs :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\init.rc:286
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	@%set PROJECT_DRIVES =  x: t: r:
	@%set found= $(PROJECT_DRIVES,M$(SB,Z))
	%if !'$(found)'
	%if ! (-e $(SB_TECH)\lib\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_TECH)\lib\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB_TECH)\inc\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_TECH)\inc\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB_TECH)\h\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_TECH)\h\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB_PRJ)\lib\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_PRJ)\lib\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(MAKETOP)\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(MAKETOP)\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB_PRJ)\h\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_PRJ)\h\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB_PRJ)\inc\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB_PRJ)\inc\$(CONFIG)\$(FLAV)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(SB)\cmds\bin\$(SYS))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(SB)\cmds\bin\$(SYS)
	%endif
	%if ! (-e $(CWD,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))\$(FLAV))
	%do mkdir_p tsb=$(SB) mdir=$(MAKETOP,$(SB_PRJ)=$(SB_PRJ)\obj\$(CONFIG))\$(FLAV)
	%endif

do_setup_file :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\depend.rc:49
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	@%set TIPATH = $(IPATH,S'$(SYSSW)\\$(COMP).*' ')
	%echo %include $(MRC)\dep.mk > $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .TYPE.obj = .obj >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .TYPE.c = .cxx .cpp .cc .c >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .TYPE.src = .asm >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .TYPE.hdr = .h .hpp .inc >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .PATH.h = $(TIPATH,W;) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .PATH.hpp = $(TIPATH,W;) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .PATH.inc = $(APATH,1);$(APATH,W;) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDRPATH.cpp = $(TIPATH) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDRPATH.cxx = $(TIPATH) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDRPATH.cc =  $(TIPATH) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDRPATH.c =   $(TIPATH) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDRPATH.asm = %(APATH,1) $(APATH) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)
	%echo .HDR.asm = ^[ \t]*[iI][nN][cC][lL][uU][dD][eE][ \t]+\([^ \t]+\) >> $(mkmf_mkfile)

end_timing :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:378
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	@%set floc = $(TMPDIR) .
	@%set secfile = $(floc,1)\$(name).tim
	@sec $($(name)_SEC) > $(secfile)
	@%set $(name)_SEC = $(secfile,@)
	@%set t_time = $($(name)_SEC) sec
	%if ! ('$(VOLUME)' < '$(vol)')
	@%echo $(str) $($(name)_SEC) sec
	%endif

flagschk :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\flags.rc:29
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	$(eko2)
	$(eko2) Performing flags check...
	%if ! %null(EXETARGS)
	%if ! %exists($(OLOC)\flags.inf)
	@touch $(OLOC)\flags.inf
	%endif
	@%set OLDFLGFILE = $(OLOC)\flags.inf
	$(@?3)%set OLDFLGS = $(OLDFLGFILE,@,W )
	$(@?3)%set NEWFLGS = $(ALL_FLAGS,W )
	%foreach flg $(NEWFLGS)
	%if !'$(OLDFLGS,M^$(flg)$$)'
	$(@?3)%set ON += $(flg)
	%endif
	%end
	%foreach flg $(OLDFLGS)
	%if !'$(NEWFLGS,M^$(flg)$$)'
	$(@?3)%set OFF += $(flg)
	%endif
	%end
	%if '$(ON)' || '$(OFF)'
	$(eko1) Turned on: $(ON)
	$(eko1) Turned off: $(OFF)
	%echo $(ON) > $(TMPDIR)\flags.dif
	%echo $(OFF) >> $(TMPDIR)\flags.dif
	%echo $(ALL_FLAGS) > $(TMPDIR)\make.flg
	%echo $(.PATH.c) > $(TMPDIR)\path.src
	%echo $(IPATH,W;) > $(TMPDIR)\path.h
	%echo $(APATH,W;) > $(TMPDIR)\path.inc
	$(@?3)%set DEFDELRSP = $(TMPDIR)\defdel.rsp
	@%echo $(OLOC) > $(DEFDELRSP)
	@%echo $(EXETARGS,<$(SYS)\\,>.dep) >> $(DEFDELRSP)
	%echo HLT is $(HLT)
	$(@?2)perl $(PERLDB) $(INIT)\defdel.pl $(TMPDIR)
	$(@?3)copy $(TMPDIR)\make.flg $(OLOC)\flags.inf
	$(eko2) Flags check complete.
	%else
	$(eko2) No flags changed.
	%endif
	%endif
	$(eko2)

freshen_lcache :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:409
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	%if $(OSVERSION) != 6
	%if ! %exists($(lcache))
	@mkdir $(lcache)
	%endif
	xcopy /D /s /e /I $(COREBACK)\$(TECH)\lib\$(SYS)\$(COMP)\$(ASM)\$(FLAV)                         $(lcache)\$(TECH)\lib\$(SYS)\$(COMP)\$(ASM)\$(FLAV)
	%else
	%do announce string="Cannot freshen lcache under DOS.  Dos is dead."
	%endif

link_rule :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\complink.rc:452
    attributes: .MISER .NODEFAULT
	@%setenv LIB=$(MAKETOP);$(LPATH,W;);$(SYSSW)\$(COMP)\LIB;$(LIB)
	$(eko1) Objects are $(FLAV), link for $(MASTER) configuration.
	%if '$(tell_libs)'
	$(eko1) Using LOCAL $(tell_libs).
	%endif
	%if %exists($(target))
	del $@
	$(eko1)         $(target,F) \<-- $(deps,F)
	%else
	$(eko1)         $(target,F) \<-- nonexistent
	%endif
	%if '$(lcache)'
	%do freshen_lcache
	%endif
	%do start_timing name=lnktime
	$(@?3)$($(COMP)_LD) $(LDFLAGS) $($(HLT)_LDFLAGS) $(filedirective) $(all_objs,>.obj,< $(oloc)\\,W\,)  $(librarydirective)          $(lib_list,W\,) $(runtime_console) $($(exet)_runtime_console) $(namedirective)$(linkspace)$@
	%if ($(VENDOR)==watcom)
	%if '$(SYS)'=='win32' && '$($(exet)_RC)'!=''
	$(@?3)$($(COMP)_RC) $(RESFLAGS) $($(exet)_RC).res $@
	%endif
	%endif
	%do end_timing vol=2 str="time:" name=lnktime
	@$(INIT)\logit $(target,F) $(t_time,S'sec'') $(INIT)\linktime.dat

mkmktmp :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:132
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	%if ! -d $(MKTMP)
	@-mkdir $(MKTMP)
	%endif
	%if ! -d $(MKTMP)
	%abort Can't create temporary directory $(MKTMP).
	%endif

mktmpdir :
    defined in: t:\prj\etc\rc\util.rc:111
    attributes: .ALWAYS .MISER .NODEFAULT .NOCOMPARE
	@%set secfile = sec.tmp
	@sec > $(secfile)
	@%set t1 = $(secfile,@)
	%if %length(t1) < 9
	%echo Can't name tmpdir, using tmptmp.tmp
	%echo Value returned from sec is $(t1)
	@%set TMPDIR=tmptmp.tmp
	%else
	@%set TMPDIR = mk$(t1,S'.*\(......\).'\1')
	%endif
	@del $(secfile)
	%if ! -d $(TMPDIR)
	@-mkdir $(TMPDIR)
	%endif
	%if ! -d $(TMPDIR)
	%abort Can't create temporary directory $(TMPDIR).
	%endif

	%endif
	%end
	%endif
	%endif
